### `RO-CLOSE-01`: Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes,…

_tier: release · status: enforced · introduced_in: PHASE4-N-V_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-V/CLOSURE.md; user-direction (PHASE4-N-V close correction) |
| **Requirement** | Unmasked close-gate discipline. Any slice that changes canonical bytes, encoded forms, decoder inputs, or golden fixtures MUST run an UNMASKED full close gate (cargo test --workspace) and use cargo's REAL exit status / result line as the sole pass/fail authority for cluster closure. Piped output (\| tail, \| grep) may be used for display only, NEVER as the pass/fail authority — a pipeline's exit code is the last stage's, not cargo's. Before closure, ALL consumers of the changed canonical output (every golden fixture, decoder, re-encode, and byte-identity test, across all crates — not just the edited crate) MUST be grepped/audited. A cluster is not closed until the unmasked close gate exits successfully. |
| **Code** | `process/release discipline — no BLUE code locus; binds /cluster-close and any slice touching canonical output` |
| **Tests** | _(no tests named in registry — gap)_ |
| **CI** | _(no CI script — gap)_ |

### `RO-LIVE-06`: BA-02 peer-acceptance evidence closure (SCHEMA + CORRELATION MECHANICS ONLY).…

_tier: release · status: enforced · introduced_in: PHASE4-N-F-C · strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-F-G-C_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/clusters/PHASE4-N-F-C/cluster.md; L6-peer-acceptance-evidence-manifest.md |
| **Requirement** | BA-02 peer-acceptance evidence closure (SCHEMA + CORRELATION MECHANICS ONLY). The BA-02 evidence surface is a closed, versioned manifest (Ba02Manifest) plus a pure, total, deterministic, HASH-PRIMARY correlator: correlate is the SOLE Ba02Manifest constructor; the forged-block hash is the REQUIRED correlation key; a peer-accept signal's slot is OPTIONAL context that must AGREE when present (a present-but-different slot contradicts -> NoEvidence); conflicting peer signals -> NoEvidence; and the peer-accept-log parser is allow-list only (peer_served_block / peer_chain_tip), dropping every weaker/self/unknown/ malformed line (ForgeSucceeded / self_accept / block_received / agreement_verdict are never coerced to acceptance). The forged evidence uses only forge-event- exposed fields (ForgedBlockArtifact.{hash,slot}); the hash is never recomputed and block bytes are never parsed. ENFORCED for the schema + correlation mechanics; NOT a claim that BA-02 was achieved live. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/ba02_evidence.rs (Ba02Manifest`, `BA02Outcome`, `PeerAcceptEvent`, `NoEvidenceReason`, `parse_peer_accept_events`, `correlate); crates/ade_node/src/ba02_pass.rs (PHASE4-N-F-G-C: RED operator-pass evidence I/O — correlate_peer_log_file reads the operator-captured peer log into the GREEN correlate; write_ba02_manifest accepts ONLY a Ba02Manifest); ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_closed.sh; ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_manifest_schema.sh` |
| **Tests** | `ba02_manifest_schema_round_trips`; `ba02_correlate_served_block_yields_manifest`; `ba02_correlate_chain_tip_only_yields_manifest`; `ba02_correlate_both_signals_agree_records_served_primary`; `ba02_correlate_served_block_without_slot_yields_manifest`; `ba02_correlate_conflicting_signals_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_correlate_wrong_hash_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_correlate_chain_point_mismatch_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_correlate_no_slot_wrong_hash_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_correlate_stale_log_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_correlate_empty_peer_log_is_no_evidence`; `ba02_self_accept_is_not_evidence`; `ba02_forge_succeeded_alone_is_not_evidence`; `ba02_block_received_alone_is_not_evidence`; `ba02_agreement_verdict_is_not_evidence`; `ba02_parser_accepts_well_formed_served_block`; `ba02_parser_drops_unknown_and_malformed_lines`; `ba02_correlate_two_runs_byte_identical`; `correlate_wired_to_operator_peer_log`; `correlate_from_operator_log_file_is_deterministic` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_closed.sh`, `ci/ci_check_ba02_evidence_manifest_schema.sh` |

### `OP-MEM-01`: Mempool pressure and peer churn must not starve block validation, chain…

| **Tests** | _(no tests named in registry — gap)_ |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_mem_measure_evidence.sh` |

_PARTIAL at MEM-MEASURE-A2 (2026-06-15). Committed live preprod transcript `docs/evidence/mem-measure-a2-preprod-memory.jsonl`: `ade_node --mode admission` warm-started from a full preprod UTxO seed (slot 125821799, epoch 295), followed the docker peer, admitted 24 blocks (24 `block_admitted` + 24 `agreement_verdict{lagging}`, 0 diverged) interleaved with 27 `memory_measure` RSS samples across 4 closed measurement points + a `memory_summary{replay_verdict=agreed}`. RSS sampling did NOT starve validation / chain selection / persistence and the run was replay-equivalent (clean exit, no fatal Diverged halt — the enforced `DC-WAL-03`); RSS magnitude never gates any authoritative output. The memory taps are observe-only seams in the admission runner (a mirror of the `--mode node` ConvergenceEvidence seams). `CI` resolves on disk; **Tests** is an explicit gap (the registry names no test fn for this operational rule — the evidence is the committed transcript validated by the CI gate, not a unit test). Flip drivers (Haskell-comparison BA-08 = MEM-COMPARE-D; `CN-MEM-01` partial→enforced live bounded queues = MEM-BOUND-B) remain. **In-span flip: `declared → partial` (this row was `declared`/gap at the `0887b2ad` baseline; MEM-MEASURE-A2 landed after it within this span).**_

### `OP-MEM-02`: Ade's owned resident memory under a representative venue stays clearly below the reference Haskell node…

_tier: operational · status: enforced · introduced_in: MEM-OPT-UTXO-DISK · cross_ref: OP-MEM-01, DC-MEM-05, DC-MEM-07_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | Project constitution §4b; bounty BA-08; MEM-OPT cluster plan (`docs/planning/mem-opt-cluster-plan.md`) |
| **Requirement** | Ade's owned resident memory (Private_Dirty/RssAnon) under a representative venue stays clearly below the reference Haskell cardano-node's on the same chain, WITHOUT changing ledger semantics, chain selection, persisted bytes, or replay-equivalence. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_node/src/mem_measure/rss_sampler.rs` (`sample_rss_anon_kib` / `sample_private_dirty_kib`), `crates/ade_ledger/src/fingerprint.rs` (`StaticUtxoFp` — compute the constant UTxO-component fingerprint ONCE, fail-closed under `track_utxo=true` / version mismatch), `crates/ade_node/src/admission/bootstrap.rs` (compute `StaticUtxoFp` before `drop(utxo)`), `ci/ci_check_utxo_fp_cache.sh`, `ci/ci_check_mem_opt_s3_owned.sh` |
| **Tests** | `owned_samplers_present_on_linux`; `static_utxo_fp_fails_closed_under_track_utxo_true_and_version_mismatch` |
| **CI** | `ci/ci_check_utxo_fp_cache.sh` (asserts `StaticUtxoFp` + the `valid_only_when_track_utxo_false` guard + `drop(utxo)` + the fail-closed `track_utxo=true` guard); `ci/ci_check_mem_opt_s3_owned.sh` (the owned-RSS measurement discipline) |

_**FLIPPED `declared → enforced` at MEM-OPT-UTXO-DISK S2b-2c.1b-A.2 (2026-06-16) — SCOPED. THIS IS THE LOAD-BEARING HONESTY NOTE; READ THE SCOPE.** `enforced` for the **CURRENT LIVE `track_utxo=false` header/tip-following admission path ONLY**: owned `RssAnon` **1.94 GiB < Haskell 2.57 GiB** on the same preprod chain — mechanically gated by `ci_check_utxo_fp_cache.sh`. The live admission runs `track_utxo=false` (it does NOT mutate the UTxO per block), so the retained 1.9M-entry in-memory UTxO was **accidental retention**, re-scanned per block to recompute a CONSTANT fingerprint. **The win is PATH A** (`StaticUtxoFp` + dropping the in-memory static UTxO, NOT the redb backend): bootstrap computes the constant UTxO-component fingerprint ONCE via `ade_ledger::fingerprint::StaticUtxoFp` (fail-closed under `track_utxo=true` / version mismatch) BEFORE `drop(utxo)`; `post_fp` uses the static component; the durable copy is the existing snapshot. Live re-measure (`docs/evidence/mem-opt-utxo-disk-s2b-2cA-owned-rss-remeasure.*`; preprod docker peer, epoch 295, fresh 3.8 GB seed): active-admission owned `RssAnon` 1.94 GiB (p50 == peak, n=33) vs Haskell 2.57 GiB → verdict `ade_below` (~25% below; 58% below the 4.59 GiB pre-A.2 baseline). Correctness: 36 blocks admitted, 1 agreed + 35 lagging, 0 diverged, 0 hash mismatches, `replay_verdict agreed` — DC-MEM-05 replay-equivalence preserved (`post_fp` byte-identical: `fingerprint_v2_with_utxo` ignores `state.utxo_state`, so the empty-UTxO live ledger == the full-UTxO `post_fp`). **NO OVER-CLAIM — the gate enforces the SCOPED owned-RSS posture, NOT the full BA-08 bounty criterion:** **(1)** enforced for the CURRENT live `track_utxo=false` path ONLY — `track_utxo=true` full live UTxO application (**LIVE-LEDGER-APPLY, "B"**) remains **OWED**; **(2)** the BOUNTY BA-08 full criterion is a **SUSTAINED ~10-day run**, certified only by that sustained measurement (**OWED**) — the current 36-block evidence POSITIONS Ade to win the 10-day window but does NOT yet certify it. Never read `enforced` here as the complete bounty criterion. All cells resolve on disk._

### `OP-OPS-04`: Operator-supplied keys. Ade supports both KES key flows: (a) Ade-native…

_tier: operational · status: enforced · strengthened_in: PHASE4-N-O, PHASE4-N-P, PHASE4-N-F-F_

| Aspect | Location |
|--------|----------|
| **Source** | docs/planning/phase4-n-c-invariants.md §7 (OQ1); docs/active/op-ops-04-ade-native-kes-flow.md; docs/planning/phase4-n-p-invariants.md |
| **Requirement** | Operator-supplied keys. Ade supports both KES key flows: (a) Ade-native `ade_node --mode key_gen_kes --out-file PATH` emitting an `ade.kes.seed.v1` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_ade_kes_signing_key`; (b) cardano-cli `node key-gen-KES` emitting a 608-byte `KesSigningKey_ed25519_kes_2^6` envelope loaded via `ade_runtime::producer::keys::load_kes_signing_key_skey`. After PHASE4-N-P S5 the cardano-cli path routes through the Ade-owned BLUE deserializer (`ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::raw_deserialize_signing_key_kes`); both flows produce a `KesSecret` whose inner is `ade_crypto::kes_sum::Sum6Kes::SigningKey` (BLUE-owned algorithm). VRF and cold (Ed25519) keys continue to be operator-supplied via cardano-cli text-envelope `.skey` files. Private-key material never crosses into BLUE — the entire RED custody surface lives under `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/{keys,signing,ade_kes_envelope}.rs`. Wrong-size payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::UnsupportedExpandedKesKeyFormat`; structurally-invalid 608-byte payloads fail-close via `KeyLoadError::KesParse(KesParseError::*)`. Mechanical enforcement: ci/ci_check_private_key_custody.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_envelope_closed.sh + ci/ci_check_kes_sum_compatibility.sh. |
| **Code** | `crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/keys.rs (load_*_signing_key_skey`, `load_ade_kes_signing_key`, `write_ade_kes_envelope`, `KeyLoadError); crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/ade_kes_envelope.rs (closed envelope grammar); crates/ade_runtime/src/producer/signing.rs (RED-confined custody`, `KesSecret with BLUE-owned inner); crates/ade_crypto/src/kes_sum/ (BLUE Sum6KES algorithm + serde + ground-truth corpus); crates/ade_node/src/key_gen.rs (one-shot key-gen-KES surface)` |

## Generation notes (prior pass — PHASE4-N-AC close)

CI: **138** (`+1` `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh`). grep / ls only; no build or test execution; the ~334 carried rows were not re-verified.

The substantive delta — **one rule introduced + enforced; one strengthened; NO existing rule weakened / re-joined / removed / deprecated; NO `RO-*` advanced** (`DC-CRYPTO-10` is a RED transmit-side key-evolution mechanism, not a Cardano semantic parameter and not a live-acceptance step — `RO-LIVE-01` stays operator-gated):

- **`DC-CRYPTO-10` — NEW, `enforced` (S1 close).** `tier = derived`, `introduced_in = "PHASE4-N-AC"`. **Source:** `docs/clusters/completed/PHASE4-N-AC/cluster.md` + `docs/evidence/c1-genesis-rehearsal-reproduction-README.md` (item-4 C1 re-run finding). The RED signing shell EVOLVES the operator KES signing key forward to the requested KES period BEFORE signing: NEW `ProducerShell::kes_sign_header_advancing(&mut self, period, preimage)` = `kes_advance_to(period)?` then `kes_sign_header`. `kes_advance_to → kes_update` is the EXISTING deterministic Sum6KES update — no-op at the current period (period-0 signing unchanged), forward-evolves in window, fail-closed `Signing(EvolutionBackwards)` on a backwards period (forward-secrecy — a destroyed past period cannot be re-signed) and `Signing(EvolutionExhausted)` beyond the key lifetime / `SUM6_MAX_PERIOD = 63`. The `period` is passed VERBATIM (no `period ± N`). The forge's single real KES sign (`produce_mode::run_real_forge_inner` step 3) now calls `kes_sign_header_advancing`; on `Err(_)` it still returns the closed `CoordinatorEvent::ForgeFailed`. The `&self` `kes_sign_at` / `kes_sign_header` REMAIN for callers that manage periods themselves. 4 on-disk tests; gate `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh` (NEW). **RED-only — 0 BLUE diff:** `git diff c6e7fafe..1d54abb4` over the BLUE `core_paths` trees touches no file and adds zero `^+(pub )?(struct|enum)` lines; the two source files changed in the whole span are both RED (`producer_shell.rs` + `produce_mode.rs`); `kes_sign_header_advancing` is a RED `&mut self` method over existing branded types — the canonical-type count is unchanged (458); `T-KEY-01` (no signing in BLUE) is preserved.
- **`CN-KES-HEADER-01` (`derived`, `strengthened_in += "PHASE4-N-AC"`).** The KES-signs-the-real-unsigned-header-pre-image invariant now ALSO covers period evolution — the signed pre-image is at the EVOLVED current period, not a stale minted-at-period-0 period. Its own four-cell contract (branded `UnsignedHeaderPreImage` + the single-source recipe + 3 tests + `ci_check_unsigned_header_preimage_single_source.sh`) is unchanged; the strengthening is the cross-period extension, not a re-scope.

**Root cause (surfaced by the C1 genesis-rehearsal re-run — recorded honestly, NOT a regression from N-U/AA/AB):** the C1 rehearsal stopped reproducing once the private net aged past one KES period (slot ~249659 / `slotsPerKESPeriod` 129600 → KES period 1), because the forge's only real KES sign called the raw `shell.kes_sign_header(kes_period, …)`, which requires `kes.current_period() == requested` — and NOTHING evolved the minted-at-period-0 operator key forward — so every leader slot failed `KesPeriodNotCurrent { requested: 1, current: 0 }` (`succeeded = 0`; the follower KeepAlive-timed-out waiting for a block). The wire/serve/intersection path was healthy. **Live proof (non-promotable rehearsal, acceptance #3):** with the fix Ade forged 3 period-1 blocks + self-accepted them, and the real cardano-node DOWNLOADED the period-1 header with NO KES/parse rejection. **Genesis-window finding (recorded honestly):** `slotsPerKESPeriod = 129600 == 3k/f = 129600`, so KES period 1 begins exactly when the genesis density window closes — a from-genesis rehearsal can never show forge-at-period-1 AND follower-adopt simultaneously; the period-1 follower rejection is `CandidateTooSparse` (genesis-density-window limit, KES-INDEPENDENT), not a KES rejection. Cross-period end-to-end forge→adopt is proven on the dense C2 tip path, NOT a net reset (which returns to period 0). Two pre-existing fail-closed INFO items handed to C2 (registry `evidence_notes`): (1) `kes_advance_to` zeroes the key on a FAILED advance — UNREACHABLE via the forge (the `kes_period_in_window` + `kes_period_for_slot` pre-check bounds the period), fail-safe; (2) the opcert window upper bound `opcert_start + 63` can diverge from the absolute Sum6KES ceiling 63 when `opcert_start > 0` (real preprod opcerts) — still fail-closed (`EvolutionExhausted`), but the C2 config must derive `kes_max_period` from the absolute ceiling.

**Registry reconciliations: NONE — 0 open on either re-traced row.** The registry `tests` / `ci_script` / `code_locus` for both N-AC rows are exact on disk (`DC-CRYPTO-10`: 4 leaf-fns + `ci_check_kes_evolution_before_sign.sh` + `kes_sign_header_advancing`/`kes_advance_to` loci + the `produce_mode.rs` call site all resolve; `CN-KES-HEADER-01`: all 3 cited leaves + the gate + loci resolve; `0` drifts).

- **`DC-NODE-12` — NEW, `enforced` (S1).** `tier = derived`. **Source:** `docs/planning/phase4-n-u-forged-block-durability-invariants.md`. Own-forged durable admit chokepoint — a self-accepted forged block becomes durable ONLY via the same `admit_forged_block_durably → pump_block` chokepoint received blocks use (`StoreBlockBytes → AppendWal → AdvanceTip`, durable-before-tip, behind the extend-only BLUE admit); bytes admitted are byte-identical to the bytes `self_accept` validated (I-10, no re-encode). Supersedes the `DC-NODE-05` "local artifact only" consequence while preserving its deeper invariant (forge advances no durable tip directly; `pump_block` is the sole durable tip authority). 3 tests, gate `ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh` (NEW) + `ci_check_node_run_loop_containment.sh` (EXTENDED in place — 2nd fenced tip-advancer allow-listed). RED-only wiring.
- **`DC-CONS-23` — NEW, `enforced` (S1).** `tier = derived`. **Source:** same sketch. Own-forged stale-tip race safety by extend-only durable admit — a stale-tip forge (forge↔feed race) FAILS CLOSED at the extend-only admit (header-position/`prev_hash`, `TipBeforeDurable`, or WAL `prior_fp`); N-U adds NO admit-time fork-choice. `DC-CONS-03` is referenced only as the boundary (it stays the follow/`chain_selector` fork-choice authority; NOT strengthened by N-U). 1 test `stale_tip_forge_fails_closed`, gate `ci_check_forged_durable_admit_via_pump.sh`.

- **`T-REC-05` — NEW, `enforced`, TEST-ENFORCED (S2).** `tier = true`. **Source:** same sketch. Replay/recovery equivalence including forged admits — same anchor + same WAL (incl. forged `AdmitBlock`) → byte-identical recovered tip + ledger fp; rides the existing snapshot + forward-replay recovery law (NO new durability law). **`ci_script = ""` by design — this is a TEST-ENFORCED true-tier rule, NOT an enforcement gap:** a forged tip carries no snapshot-at-tip, so `warm_start_recovery` forward-replays from the genesis slot-0 snapshot over the durable WAL block under a fingerprint fail-fast guard (recovered fp == WAL-tail `post_fp`); reaching `Ok` with the same tip IS byte-identical equivalence, proven by `forge_kill_then_warm_start_recovers_same_tip_via_forward_replay` (riding the already-CI-gated `bootstrap_initial_state` warm-start branch). 1 test.

Served view is a durable-chain projection — the `--mode node` ChainView (ChainSync header / BlockFetch body) is a deterministic read-only PROJECTION of the durable ChainDb (`ChainDbServedSource` over `&dyn ChainDb`, serving `stored.bytes` verbatim via the single `block_header_bytes` / DC-CONS-18 authority); a follower fetches coherent history A→B, never B without A.
